# Supplementary Table 10. Differentially expressed genes of subsets within major cell lineages
# Differentially expressed genes for each cluster analyzed within each major cell lineage (Cancer epithelial, Normal Epithelial, T-cells, B-cells, Myeloid, CAFs, PVL and Endothelial). Subset level clusters were compared against all other clusters within their major lineage using the MAST method (FindAllMarkers) with a log-scale fold change threshold of 0.25, detected in at least 0.1 of cells in either clusters and genes with a fraction difference of 0.1. Genes were filtered by an adjusted p-value threshold of 0.05. Statistical significance for differential gene expression in MAST69 was determined using the wilcox test, with all p-values adjusted using bonferroni correction.
